# Current App + Preserved Architecture Research Packet — 2026-05-08

Generated from `/Users/jojo/Downloads/Epistemos` after filtering out extra Helios research/sprawl. This is the packet to use for current app work plus the architecture upgrades that are meant to survive in the app.

## Scope

- Total linked current-app code/config/test files: **1867**.
- Total 20-file research batches: **106**.
- Includes live Swift app code, Swift tests, current Rust runtime crates, graph engine, SCOPE-Rex/Resonance preserved architecture files inside `agent_core`, JS editor, XPC/helper/widget code, local package sources, current tools/scripts, CLI passthrough surfaces, and local/cloud agent routing code.
- Excludes raw Helios docs/corpora, `epistemos-research/`, `epistemos-vault/`, `lean/`, `Tools/falsifier/`, `Tools/sorry-budget/`, `Tools/forensic-cite/`, generated outputs, archived worktrees, temp folders, node_modules, target dirs, DerivedData, and Helios-only app scaffolds (`HELIOSv5SettingsView.swift`, `HELIOSInvariantSourceGuardTests.swift`).
- This packet classifies excluded scaffolds; it does not delete them.

## Tool And Command Surface Reconciliation

- **Main chat slash commands:** 13 built-in presets from `ACCSlashCommand`: `/ask`, `/notes`, `/code`, `/debug`, `/plan`, `/research`, `/review`, `/security-review`, `/summarize`, `/read-branch`, `/explain`, `/todo`, `/image`.
- **Omega MCP built-in tools:** 40 registered definitions: 33 from `omega-mcp/src/catalog.rs` plus 7 graph verbs from `omega-mcp/src/graph_tools.rs`.
- **LocalAgent compatibility catalog:** 107 declared command/tool patterns: 81 core, 24 pro, 2 research. This is a compatibility inventory, not proof that every pattern is live in the main chat.
- **Agent Core tool registry:** separate Rust runtime catalog with tier filtering, build gating, explicit allowlists, and Swift bridging through `ToolTierBridge`.

Audit rule: never compare slash command count directly to tool count. For each item, answer: where is it advertised, where is it parsed, where is it executed, what build/tier can see it, what approval gate protects it, what success/failure does the user see, and what test proves the path.

## User-Facing Feature Audit Mandate

The research pass must find features that were half-built, hidden, or unusable. For every feature, produce this ledger:

| Field | Required answer |
|---|---|
| Feature name | User-facing name, not internal class name. |
| Entry point | Menu, toolbar, slash command, settings row, contextual button, keyboard shortcut, file association, background trigger, or none. |
| Runtime path | Exact caller chain from UI/input to state/service/FFI/tool/provider. |
| Capability gate | Build flag, entitlement, API key, model availability, vault permission, App Store policy, network, subprocess, or none. |
| User proof | Manual steps a user can take today, expected visible result, and failure state. |
| Test proof | Unit/integration/UI/manual/log evidence. |
| Classification | visible-working, visible-broken, hidden-working, hidden-dead, feature-gated, implemented-not-wired, or excluded-speculative. |

Do not mark anything done because it has a model, view, registry entry, source guard, or test fixture. It is done only if a user can reach it or it is intentionally hidden behind a documented gate.

## Current-App Deep Research Prompt

```text
You are auditing the current Epistemos app, not the speculative Helios research archive. Cover only live product code plus architecture upgrades that are intended to be preserved in the current app. Treat research/vault/Lean/extra Helios scaffolds as out-of-scope unless a current product file imports or displays them.

Rules:
1. Start with AGENTS.md, CLAUDE.md, docs/fusion/MASTER_RESEARCH_INDEX_2026_05_02.md, docs/SUBSTRATE_V2_FINAL_CLOSEOUT_2026_05_05.md, docs/audits/PRE_HELIOS_FEATURE_AUDIT_2026_05_06.md, docs/HELIOS_V5_INTEGRATION_PLAN_v2_2026_05_05.md, and docs/HELIOS_V5_INTEGRATION_PLAN_v2_FINALIZE_2026_05_05.md. Use the Helios docs only to decide preserved/current vs speculative/excluded.
2. Do not audit the raw Helios research corpus, epistemos-research, epistemos-vault, Lean theorem stubs, falsifier protocols, or Helios settings/source-guard scaffolds as current app code. Mention them only in the exclusion ledger.
3. For every preserved architecture item, assign one of: current-wired, implemented-not-wired, feature-gated, scaffold-only, not-implemented, excluded-speculative.
4. For each 20-file batch, read every file and produce a dossier: purpose, public API, state ownership, threading/actor model, persistence, FFI boundary, hot paths, security/privacy, error handling, existing tests, missing tests, and cross-file callers/callees found with rg.
5. Trace current app flows end to end: note/editor save, .epdoc graph/image projection, Halo/shadow search, graph render, slash commands, Omega MCP tools, local agent/tool execution, CLI passthrough agents, cloud agent tool loops, DAG/replay/provenance, SovereignGate/capability grants, Live Notes, LSP, XPC, and model/provider routing.
6. Verify preserved architecture invariants without accepting names as proof: AnswerPacket must be emitted by chat to be wired; Rust modules without Swift/CI/UI callers are implemented-not-wired; source-guard-only tests are not runtime evidence.
7. Every finding needs file links and line-level evidence. Every "implemented" claim must name the code path, caller, test, and runtime visibility surface.
8. Reconcile command/tool counts. Main chat slash commands, Omega MCP tools, LocalAgent compatibility commands, and Agent Core tool schemas are different inventories; prove where each one is advertised, parsed, executed, gated, and surfaced to the user.
9. Identify half-built or hidden features. Every feature must receive one of: visible-working, visible-broken, hidden-working, hidden-dead, feature-gated, implemented-not-wired, scaffold-only, not-implemented, excluded-speculative.
10. Finish with a coverage ledger, implementation matrix, command/tool reconciliation ledger, user-facing reachability ledger, excluded-speculation ledger, and next audit/fix tasks.
```

## Implementation Classification Rules

- **current-wired**: live code path has caller, test, and visible/auditable runtime surface.
- **implemented-not-wired**: types/functions/tests exist, but production caller or UI/runtime emission is missing.
- **feature-gated**: code exists behind `pro-build`, `research`, settings toggles, App Store conditionals, or entitlement gates.
- **scaffold-only**: source guard, placeholder, or isolated crate exists without product integration.
- **not-implemented**: canon describes it, but no current product code exists.
- **excluded-speculative**: intentionally out of this packet: research/vault/Lean/falsifier/raw Helios material.

## Suggested Audit Order

1. Current app bootstrap and environment.
2. Models, MutationEnvelope, AnswerPacket, provenance, EventStore, and Cognitive DAG.
3. Note editor, `.epdoc`, graph projection, vault sync, and Halo/shadow search.
4. Main chat slash commands, Omega MCP catalog, LocalAgent compatibility commands, Agent Core tiered tools, CLI passthrough agents, and cloud agent tool loop.
5. SovereignGate, CapabilityBridge, XPC, LSP, and Live Notes.
6. Graph Swift layer plus Rust graph engine/FFI.
7. Knowledge Fusion and subprocess-debt audit.
8. User-facing feature reachability audit across menus/settings/toolbars/shortcuts/background triggers.
9. Tests and CI proof map.
